It operates through the following segments: North America, International, and Amazon Web Services (AWS). The North America segment is involved in the retail sales of consumer products including from sellers and subscriptions through North America-focused online and physical stores. It also includes export sales from online stores. The AWS segment consists of global sales of compute, storage, database, and other services for start-ups, enterprises, government agencies, and academic institutions. \n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\n\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class="spacer-50 mobile-spacer-25"></div>\n\t\t<div class="graviton">\n\t\t\t<h2 class="header-underline">The History of Amazon\xe2\x80\x99s Stock Price by Markets Insider</h2>\n            <div class="instrument-description instrument-description--profile">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a href="https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon">Amazon</a>. com, Inc. is a multinational technology company, which engages in the provision of online retail shopping services. It operates through the following segments: North America, International, and Amazon Web Services (<a href="https://www.businessinsider.com/aws">AWS</a>).
